<script>document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){
function moveElements() {
if (window.innerWidth >= 768) {
let tableRows = document.querySelectorAll('.myhikaku tbody tr');
tableRows.forEach(row => {
let cell1 = row.querySelector('.cell1'); // 最初のtd選択
row.appendChild(cell1); // cell1を最後に移動
});
let headerRows = document.querySelectorAll('.myhikaku thead tr');
headerRows.forEach(headerRow => {
let header2 = headerRow.querySelector('.header2');
headerRow.appendChild(header2); // header2を最後に移動
});
}
}
window.addEventListener('resize', moveElements);
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', moveElements); // ページロード時にも条件を確認して適用});</script>

}
});
});
});

{ src: 'https://iinecash.com/genkinka/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/linemo_card.webp', alt: 'LINEMO', value: 'linemo' }
]
};
function cardImagesHtml(site) {
const creditImages = tabCardImageMap.credit || [];
const atobaraiImages = tabCardImageMap.atobarai || [];
const carrierImages = tabCardImageMap.carrier || [];
const creditFiltered = creditImages.filter(img =>
site.cards?.includes(img.value)
);
const atobaraiFiltered = atobaraiImages.filter(img =>
site.cards?.includes(img.value)
);
const carrierFiltered = carrierImages.filter(img =>
site.cards?.includes(img.value)
);
let html = '';
if (creditFiltered.length > 0) {
html += `
<div class="row3 yuryo">対応ブランド</div>
<div class="row4 yuryo">
<div>
<ul class="card-list">
${creditFiltered.map(img => `
<li class="detail-cards">
<img decoding="async" src="${img.src}" alt="${img.alt}" class="card-icon" />
</li>`).join('')}
</ul>
</div>
</div>`;
}
if (atobaraiFiltered.length > 0 || carrierFiltered.length > 0) {
html += `
<div class="row3">
${atobaraiFiltered.length > 0 ? `<div>対応アプリ</div>` : ''}
${carrierFiltered.length > 0 ? `<div class="item2">対応キャリア</div>` : ''}
${atobaraiFiltered.length > 0 ? `
<div class="item3">
<ul class="card-list">
${atobaraiFiltered.map(img => `
<li class="detail-cards">
<img decoding="async" src="${img.src}" alt="${img.alt}" class="card-icon" />
</li>
`).join('')}
</ul>
</div>` : ''}
${carrierFiltered.length > 0 ? `
<div>
<ul class="card-list">
${carrierFiltered.map(img => `
<li class="detail-cards">
<img decoding="async" src="${img.src}" alt="${img.alt}" class="card-icon" />
</li>
`).join('')}
</ul>
</div>` : ''}
</div>
`;
}
return html;
}
const tabButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');
const cardSectionLabel = document.getElementById('card-section-label');
const cardButtonsContainer = document.getElementById('card-buttons-container');
const amountButtonsContainer = document.getElementById('amount-buttons-container');
const priorityButtonsContainer = document.getElementById('priority-buttons-container');
const filteredCountElem = document.getElementById('filtered-count');
const btnReset = document.getElementById('btn-reset');
const btnShow = document.getElementById('btn-show');
const modalOverlay = document.getElementById('result-modal');
const modalCloseBtn = document.getElementById('modal-close');
const modalList = document.getElementById('modal-list');
const modalPagination = document.getElementById('modal-pagination');
const ITEMS_PER_PAGE = 5;
let currentPage = 1;
let currentResults = [];
function getAmountNumber(amountStr) {
if (!amountStr) return 0;
return parseInt(
amountStr
.replace('万円〜', '')
.replace('万円', '')
.replace('万〜', '')
.replace('万', '')
.replace('円', '')
.trim()
);
}
function countStars(ratingStr) {
return (ratingStr.match(/★/g) || []).length;
}
function filterAndRenderResults() {
if (selectedCards.size === 0 && !selectedAmount && selectedPriorities.size === 0) {
filteredCountElem.textContent = 0;
currentResults = [];
modalList.innerHTML = '';
modalPagination.innerHTML = '';
return;
}
const currentCategoryId = tabCategoryMap[currentTab];
const filtered = siteData.filter(site => {
// カテゴリフィルター
if (!site.category || ![].concat(site.category).some(cat => String(cat) === String(currentCategoryId))) {
return false;
}
// カードフィルター
if (
selectedCards.size > 0 &&
![...selectedCards].every(card =>
site.cards && site.cards.includes(card)
)
) {
return false;
}
// 金額フィルター
if (selectedAmount && site.amount?.trim() !== selectedAmount.trim()) {
return false;
}
// 優先順位フィルター
if (selectedPriorities.size > 0) {
const sitePriorities = Array.isArray(site.priority) ? site.priority : [];
for (const priority of selectedPriorities) {
if (!sitePriorities.includes(priority)) {
return false;
}
}
}
return true;
});
// 星数基準降順整列
filtered.sort((a, b) => countStars(b.rating) - countStars(a.rating));
filteredCountElem.textContent = filtered.length;
currentResults = filtered;
currentPage = 1;
renderModalPage(currentPage);
}
function renderCardButtons() {
cardButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
cardSectionLabel.textContent = cardData[currentTab].label;
cardData[currentTab].cards.forEach(card => {
const btn = document.createElement('button');
btn.type = 'button';
btn.title = card.alt;
btn.dataset.value = card.value;
const img = document.createElement('img');
img.src = card.src;
img.alt = card.alt;
btn.appendChild(img);
btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
const clickedValue = e.currentTarget.dataset.value;
if (selectedCards.has(clickedValue)) {
selectedCards.delete(clickedValue);
} else {
selectedCards.add(clickedValue);
}
updateCardButtonStates();
filterAndRenderResults();
});
cardButtonsContainer.appendChild(btn);
});
updateCardButtonStates();
}
function updateCardButtonStates() {
const buttons = cardButtonsContainer.querySelectorAll('button');
buttons.forEach(btn => {
const value = btn.dataset.value;
if (selectedCards.has(value)) {
btn.classList.add('selected');
} else {
btn.classList.remove('selected');
}
});
}
function renderAmountButtons() {
amountButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
amountOptions.forEach(amount => {
const btn = document.createElement('button');
btn.type = 'button';
btn.textContent = amount;
btn.dataset.value = amount;
btn.className = selectedAmount === amount ? 'selected' : '';
btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
selectedAmount = selectedAmount === amount ? null : amount;
renderAmountButtons();
filterAndRenderResults();
});
amountButtonsContainer.appendChild(btn);
});
}
function renderPriorityButtons() {
priorityButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
priorityOptions.forEach(priority => {
const btn = document.createElement('button');
btn.type = 'button';
btn.textContent = priority;
btn.dataset.value = priority;
btn.className = selectedPriorities.has(priority) ? 'selected' : '';
btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
if (selectedPriorities.has(priority)) selectedPriorities.delete(priority);
else selectedPriorities.add(priority);
renderPriorityButtons();
filterAndRenderResults();
});
priorityButtonsContainer.appendChild(btn);
});
}
function renderColoredStars(ratingStr) {
const stars = ratingStr.split('').map(star => {
const isFilled = star === '★';
return `<span class="star ${isFilled ? 'filled' : ''}">${star}</span>`;
}).join('');
return `<div class="star-rating">${stars}</div>`;
}
function renderModalPage(page) {
modalList.innerHTML = '';
const start = (page - 1) * ITEMS_PER_PAGE;
const end = start + ITEMS_PER_PAGE;
const pageItems = currentResults.slice(start, end);
currentResults.forEach((site, index) => {
const pageNum = Math.floor(index / ITEMS_PER_PAGE) + 1;
const isCurrentPage = pageNum === page;
// 現在ページ以外の項目にはnoindexメタタグ追加
if (!isCurrentPage) {
const meta = document.createElement('meta');
meta.name = 'robots';
meta.content = 'noindex';
document.head.appendChild(meta);
}
});
pageItems.forEach(site => {
const item = document.createElement('div');
item.className = 'site-item';
item.innerHTML = `
<h3><a href="${site.url}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">${site.name}</a></h3>
<div class="modal-info">
<div class="detail-l">
<div class="detail-img"><span class="jump" data-label="button" data-id="${site.id}" role="button"><img decoding="async" src="${site.img}" alt="${site.name}" /></span></div>
<div class="detail-rating">${renderColoredStars(site.rating)}</div>
</div>
<div class="site-info">
<div class="custom-table">
<div class="row1">スピード</div>
<div class="row1">換金率</div>
<div class="row1">利用可能額</div>
<div class="row2">${currentTab === 'credit' ? `最短${site.speed}分` : site.speed}</div>
<div class="row2">${currentTab === 'credit' ? `${site.kankin}%` : site.kankin}</div>
<div class="row2">${site.gaku}</div>
${cardImagesHtml(site)}
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="site-tags">
<div class="site-tags-list">
${
priorityOptions.map(tag => {
const isSelected = Array.isArray(site.priority) && site.priority.includes(tag);
const label = priorityLabelMap[tag] || tag;
return `<span class="priority-tag${isSelected ? ' selected' : ''}">${label}</span>`;
}).join(' ')
}
</div>
</div>
<p>${site.campain}</p>
<div class="mo-btn-cv">
<span class="mo-btn-cv-icon">
<svg class="iconArrowRight" width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M10 6L15.2929 11.2929C15.6834 11.6834 15.6834 12.3166 15.2929 12.7071L10 18" stroke="#ffffff" stroke-linecap="round"></path>
</svg>
</span>
<span class="jump" data-label="button" data-id="${site.id}" role="button" tabindex="0"><span class="mo_link_bt">公式サイトを見る</span></span>
</div>
`;
modalList.appendChild(item);
});
modalPagination.innerHTML = '';
const totalPages = Math.ceil(currentResults.length / ITEMS_PER_PAGE);
if (totalPages <= 1) return;
for (let i = 1; i <= totalPages; i++) {
const pageBtn = document.createElement('button');
pageBtn.textContent = i;
pageBtn.className = (i === page) ? 'active' : '';
pageBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
currentPage = i;
renderModalPage(i);
});
modalPagination.appendChild(pageBtn);
}
}
tabButtons.forEach(btn => {
btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
tabButtons.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
btn.classList.add('active');
currentTab = btn.dataset.tab;
selectedCards.clear();
renderCardButtons();
filterAndRenderResults();
});
});
btnReset.addEventListener('click', () => {
selectedCards.clear();
selectedAmount = null;
selectedPriorities.clear();
currentPage = 1;
renderCardButtons();
renderAmountButtons();
renderPriorityButtons();
filterAndRenderResults();
});
btnShow.addEventListener('click', () => {
filterAndRenderResults();
modalOverlay.style.display = 'flex';
});
modalCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
modalOverlay.style.display = 'none';
});
// 初期表示
renderCardButtons();
renderAmountButtons();
renderPriorityButtons();
filterAndRenderResults();
})();
</script>
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
const titles = document.querySelectorAll('.c-widget__title.-footer');
titles.forEach(title => {
const list = title.nextElementSibling?.querySelector('.lcp_catlist');
if (title && list) {
title.addEventListener('click', function() {
this.classList.toggle('active');
list.classList.toggle('expanded');
});
}
});
});
</script>
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
const tocBtn = document.getElementById('toc-label-btn');
const topBtn = document.getElementById('pagetop-mobile');
const modal = document.getElementById('toc-modal');
const modalBody = document.getElementById('toc-modal-body');
const closeBtn = document.querySelector('.toc-modal-close');
const fixBtns = document.querySelector('.mobile-fix-buttons');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
if (window.scrollY > 100) {
fixBtns?.classList.add('show');
} else {
fixBtns?.classList.remove('show');
}
});
function waitForToc(selector, callback, interval = 100, timeout = 5000) {
const startTime = Date.now();
(function check() {
const el = document.querySelector(selector);
if (el) {
callback(el);
} else if (Date.now() - startTime < timeout) {
setTimeout(check, interval);
} else {
console.log('Timeout waiting for TOC');
}
})();
}
waitForToc('.p-toc__list.is-style-index', () => {
});
const swellTocList = document.querySelector('.p-toc__list');
if (!swellTocList) {
console.log('Swell TOC not found on page.');
}
tocBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
modalBody.innerHTML = '';
const swellTocList = document.querySelector('.p-toc__list');
if (swellTocList) {
const clonedToc = swellTocList.cloneNode(true);
clonedToc.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(a => {
a.addEventListener('click', e => {
e.preventDefault();
const targetId = a.getAttribute('href').slice(1);
const targetEl = document.getElementById(targetId);
if (targetEl) {
targetEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
}
modal.classList.remove('active');
});
});
modalBody.appendChild(clonedToc);
} else {
modalBody.innerHTML = '<p>目次が見つかりませんでした。</p>';
}
modal.classList.add('active');
});
function closeModal() {
modal.classList.remove('active');
}
closeBtn?.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
modal?.addEventListener('click', e => {
if (e.target === modal) closeModal();
});
topBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
});
});
</script>
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
const tabMenus = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-menu');
tabMenus.forEach(menu => {
const buttons = menu.querySelectorAll('.tab-button');
const container = menu.nextElementSibling; // .tab-content-area
const tabs = container.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');
buttons.forEach(button => {
button.addEventListener('click', () => {
const target = button.dataset.tab;
buttons.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
button.classList.add('active');
const tabToShow = container.querySelector('#' + target);
if (tabToShow) tabToShow.classList.add('active');
});
});
});
});
</script>
